                def meets_height_requirements?(user_height, containing_wall_height)

                  # EN 14960:2019 - Containing wall heights must scale with user height: no walls <0.6m, equal height 0.6-3m, 1.25x height 3-6m, plus permanent roof >6m

              def self.create_pdf_table(pdf, data)
          
      148. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    148. 
            

            

                table = pdf.table(data, width: pdf.bounds.width) do |t|
          
      149. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    149. 
            

            

                  t.cells.borders = []
          
      150.

      151. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    151. 
            

            

                  t.columns(0).font_style = :bold
          
      152. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    152. 
            

            

                  t.columns(0).width = 150
          
      153. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    153. 
            

            

                  t.row(0..data.length - 1).background_color = "EEEEEE"
          
      154. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    154. 
            

            

                  t.row(0..data.length - 1).borders = [:bottom]
          
      155. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    155. 
            

            

                  t.row(0..data.length - 1).border_color = "DDDDDD"
          
      156. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    156. 
            

            

                end
          
      157. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    157. 
            

            

            
          
      158. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    158. 
            

            

                yield table if block_given?

                table

              def self.generate_qr_code_from_url(url)
